Have you estimated whether the ISS metastable vacuum has a cosmologically acceptable lifetime for the parameter values relevant to QCD?

results/brainstorm_r15.md:166:Yes, through the Yukawa couplings W_Yukawa = y_c H_u M^d_d + y_b H_d M^s_s. These couple the Higgs sector to the meson sector regardless of whether X = S. The ISS flavor-universality identity y_j <M_j> = 2C/v holds, ensuring that the Higgs F-terms are flavor-blind. The meson-Higgs couplings still transmit SUSY breaking from the meson sector to the Higgs sector, generating soft masses of order F/v ~ C/v^2 ~ 10^{-2} MeV (far too small to be the dominant SUSY-breaking source).

results/combined_vacuum.md-133-1. **Seiberg's result (1994):** For N_f = N_c, the low-energy description is in terms of gauge-invariant composites M, B, B~ subject to the quantum modified constraint det M - BB~ = Lambda^{2N_c}. The Lagrange multiplier X enforces this constraint. It has no kinetic term.
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/combined_vacuum.md-134-
results/combined_vacuum.md:135:2. **No magnetic dual:** Seiberg duality maps N_f = N_c to N_c' = N_f - N_c = 0. There is no magnetic gauge group. The ISS mechanism requires N_f > N_c to produce a dynamical pseudo-modulus. For N_f = N_c, there is no magnetic theory and no dynamical X.
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/combined_vacuum.md-136-
results/combined_vacuum.md-137-3. **Smooth quantum moduli space:** The constraint det M - BB~ = Lambda^6 defines a smooth variety (no singularities). The instanton-generated ADS superpotential W_dyn = Lambda^{2N_c+1}/det M enforces this at the quantum level.

results/kahler_leptons.md:130:## 5. Why the Kähler Cannot Generate Lepton Masses
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-131-
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-132-### 5a. The rank obstruction
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-133-
results/kahler_leptons.md:134:The 4-field system (M_u, M_d, M_s, X) gives W_IJ of rank 2 (one nonzero Dirac pair). Including the two Higgs fields (H_u, H_d) extends this to rank 6, giving three Dirac pairs. Kähler rescaling is a congruence transformation K^{-1/2} W K^{-1/2} and preserves the rank exactly. No Kähler correction can generate masses for states that are massless at tree level.
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-135-
results/kahler_leptons.md-136-### 5b. Scale mismatch: X sector
--
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-144-    K_{M_s M_s} ~ (W_{M_s X} * Lambda / m_tau)^2 = 2.27e+06
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-145-
results/kahler_leptons.md:146:This requires c_s ~ 10^5 in K = |M_s|^2 + c_s |M_s|^4/Lambda^2. A value c_s >> 1 is outside the domain of validity of any Kähler expansion.
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-147-
results/kahler_leptons.md-148-### 5c. Scale mismatch: Yukawa sector
--
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-153-    y_b * Lambda = 10.19 MeV  (should be m_mu = 105.7 MeV)
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-154-
results/kahler_leptons.md:155:These are wrong by factors of 6 and 10, respectively, in opposite directions. A Kähler suppression can reduce y_c * Lambda toward m_e, but simultaneously reduces y_b * Lambda further away from m_mu. The ratio m_mu / m_e = 206.8 requires:
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-156-
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-157-    K_d / K_s = (y_c / y_b)^2 * (m_mu / m_e)^2 = (0.304)^2 * (206.8)^2 = 3945
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-158-
results/kahler_leptons.md:159:This ratio of Kähler metrics is achievable in principle, but it does not produce Q = 2/3 (the resulting Q is approximately 0.35 in the Yukawa-dominated limit).
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-160-
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-161-### 5d. Asymptotic behavior of Q
--
results/kahler_leptons.md-163-In the limit where X is completely suppressed (K_X -> infinity), the remaining two Yukawa masses become exactly degenerate in pairs: (y_b * Lambda / sqrt(K_s), y_b * Lambda / sqrt(K_s)) and (y_c * Lambda / sqrt(K_d), y_c * Lambda / sqrt(K_d)). The three largest singular values are a degenerate pair from the X sector (suppressed by K_X) and y_b / sqrt(K_s). The Koide ratio of three such masses approaches 1/3 (degenerate limit) or 1/2 (one pair + one distinct), never 2/3.
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-164-
results/kahler_leptons.md:165:Numerically: the best Q found scanning all four Kähler parameters is Q = 0.499 ~ 1/2, not 2/3.
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-166-
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-167----
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-168-
results/kahler_leptons.md:169:## 6. The Role of Bion Kähler in This Framework
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-170-
results/kahler_leptons.md:171:The bion Kähler K_bion = (epsilon/Lambda^2)|sum_k s_k sqrt(M_k)|^2 has the correct interpretation for the QUARK sector, not the lepton sector:
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-172-
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-173-1. At the SUSY vacuum M_i = Lambda^2/m_i, the bion correction is O(epsilon * m_i/Lambda^2) -- negligible.

/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-193-## 8. Conclusion
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-194-
results/kahler_leptons.md:195:**Bion-induced Kähler corrections cannot generate a lepton-like spectrum from the tree-level W_IJ at the Seiberg vacuum.**
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-196-
results/kahler_leptons.md-197-The obstructions are structural and scale-based:
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-198-
results/kahler_leptons.md:199:**(1) Rank invariance.** The number of nonzero fermion masses is fixed by the rank of W_IJ. Kähler corrections are congruence transformations (K^{-1/2} W K^{-1/2}) and cannot change the rank. With the given superpotential, one gets three Dirac pairs -- not the issue -- but their hierarchy is determined by W_IJ, not K.
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-200-
results/kahler_leptons.md:201:**(2) Wrong scales.** The X-sector masses are Lambda^5/(m_j m_k) ~ 10^4 - 10^6 MeV, far above the lepton scale. The Yukawa-sector masses are y * Lambda ~ 3 - 10 MeV, also far from (0.511, 105.7, 1776.9) MeV. No natural Kähler correction bridges these gaps without extreme fine-tuning (c_i ~ 10^5 for the strange-quark sector).
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-202-
results/kahler_leptons.md:203:**(3) Q does not reach 2/3.** A complete scan over all flavor-dependent Kähler parameters finds Q in the range [0.35, 0.50]. The value Q = 2/3 is not approached. This is a consequence of the fact that the Koide condition on leptons is not a consequence of the mass formula W_IJ / sqrt(K_{II} K_{JJ}) with this W_IJ.
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-204-
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-205-**(4) Bion suppression is too small.** At the Seiberg vacuum, delta_K_{ij} ~ epsilon * sqrt(m_i m_j)/Lambda^2 ~ 10^{-7} to 10^{-6}. Mass corrections are at the sub-percent level and cannot produce order-of-magnitude hierarchies.
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/kahler_leptons.md-206-
results/kahler_leptons.md:207:**The correct role of K_bion in this theory:** The bion Kähler generates the effective potential V_mon ~ |S_bloom - 2*S_seed|^2 whose minimum gives the v0-doubling relation sqrt(m_b) = 3*sqrt(m_s) + sqrt(m_c). results/assembly_round7.md-77-4. **Six tachyonic scalar modes**: R-components of us and ds off-diagonal mesons (m² = −62384 and −144713 MeV²), plus 2 central-block R modes. The holomorphic mass contribution W_{IJK}F_I overcomes the positive soft mass f_π². This signals the diagonal vacuum ansatz is NOT the true minimum when Yukawas + EWSB are included.
/home/codexssh/phys3/results/assembly_round7.md-78-
results/assembly_round7.md:79:5. **Supertrace exact**: STr[M²] = 2 Tr(M²_soft) = 18 f_π² = 152352 MeV². The W² piece cancels between scalar and fermion sectors.
